# Pre-Launch Refactor Spec

> **Status:** Implemented — data layer + extraction shipped 2026-04-29; module
> carve, strict types, Vite, and production cutover (Cloudflare Pages)
> completed 2026-05-02. § 13 lives on as the project-wide decisions log.
> **Author:** Adam Denney (AI-assisted)
> **Date:** written 2026-04-28 · body reconciled with shipped reality 2026-06-11

This spec covered the structural work done **before launch**: moving app
data off localStorage into Postgres, splitting the god file into modules, and
adding a build step. §§ 1–12 are the historical contract, now annotated with
what actually shipped (including deviations). It does not cover post-launch
features — those live in `PLAN.md` and accrue entries in § 13.

Companion docs:
- `PLAN.md` — central planning doc (current work, sub-steps, status)
- `SCHEMA.md` — full database schema (drafted 2026-04-27; source of truth)
- `index.html` — now an ~840-line markup shell; the ~11,400-line god file this
  spec describes was split into `src/*.js` (see § 10 / § 13)

---

## 1. Problem

ProCabinet works as a prototype but is structured for throwaway code, not for
launch:

- **Data is split between Supabase and localStorage**, with most app data
  (sheets, pieces, edge bands, cabinets, quote lines, catalogs, biz info) in
  localStorage. This means: no multi-device sync, no backups, no real reports,
  no path to teams.
- **The codebase is one 11,430-line `index.html`** with 408 functions, 369
  inline event handlers, and ~30 top-level mutable globals. Every change
  touches the same file; every typo can break unrelated features.
- **Two parallel subsystems exist** (Cabinet Builder + Cabinet Quote) with
  overlapping schemas — clarity debt that will only compound.

> *(Historical — describes the app as of 2026-04-28. All three problems were
> resolved: data lives in Postgres, the god file is split into `src/*.js`, and
> the two cabinet subsystems were unified post-launch — § 13, 2026-05-05.)*

---

## 2. Why now

- **Pre-launch is the only free window for schema changes.** Once real users
  have real data, every column rename is a migration with risk.
- **The god file's pain compounds per feature.** Every new feature added now
  is one more thing to detangle later.
- **AI-assisted iteration is materially faster on modular code** — the
  workflow you already use benefits directly from this refactor.

> *(As it played out: the refactor ran 2026-04-28 → 2026-05-02, immediately
> before go-live, and the "only free window" bet held — every schema change
> since launch has been an additive migration.)*

---

## 3. Goals (in priority order)

1. **All app data persists in Postgres** — zero functional data in
   localStorage (UI prefs only).
2. **Code is split into feature modules** under ~1000 lines each, no god file.
3. **A new feature can be prototyped in one file** without touching the rest
   of the app.
4. **The app supports cross-project queries** ("most-used cabinet sizes",
   "edge banding consumed YTD") via real SQL.
5. **Deployment works end-to-end** on a real domain with auth, with no manual
   localStorage seeding.

> *(All five delivered — see § 7 for verification. #2's "~1000 lines each"
> was relaxed in practice; see the file-size note in § 7.)*

---

## 4. Non-goals (explicit)

These are tempting but **out of scope**:

- Switching to React / Vue / Svelte (vanilla JS stays)
- Adding new features during the refactor
- Writing tests retroactively (smoke testing only)
- Multi-user / team support (single-user-per-account stays)
- Mobile native app
- Rewriting cut-list optimization algorithm
- Public API or third-party integrations
- Perfect code — "good enough to launch" is the bar

> *(All held through the refactor and launch. Post-launch, several were
> deliberately revisited as features, not scope creep: Builder/Quote
> unification (2026-05-05), nested CNC cut optimization (2026-05-25),
> QuickBooks/Xero + Stripe integrations (2026-05-30 / 2026-06-09) — § 13.
> Still standing: vanilla JS, no tests, single-user accounts, no native app.)*

---

## 5. Constraints

| Constraint | Value (as shipped) |
|---|---|
| Time budget | Actual: ~5 days — 2026-04-28 → 2026-05-02 production cutover |
| Tech stack | Vanilla JS, Supabase Postgres, no framework |
| Build step | Yes — Vite (added 2026-04-30, reversing the initial defer; § 13) |
| Downtime tolerance | Was pre-launch/unlimited; moot since the 2026-05-02 cutover |
| Solo or assisted | Solo + AI-assisted |
| Browser support | Modern evergreen; mobile Safari via the responsive pass (2026-05-23) |
| Hosting | Cloudflare Pages (`procabinet.app`), auto-deploy from `main` — not the Netlify option PLAN.md originally floated |

---

## 6. Scope

### In scope

- [x] Database schema redesign (per `SCHEMA.md`) — 2026-04-28
- [x] Migrate all localStorage data to Postgres tables — 2026-04-28
- [x] Extract CSS to `styles.css` — 2026-04-28
- [x] Split JS under `src/` — completed 2026-05-01 as a **classic-script
      carve**, not ES modules (deliberate deviation, § 13 2026-04-30; only
      `main.js` is a module)
- [x] `window.X` exports for inline handlers — moot under the classic-script
      split: functions stay in the shared global lexical environment, typed
      via `src/globals.d.ts`
- [x] ~~Convert global mutable state to a shared `state` object~~ — dropped;
      strict-mode JSDoc typing over cross-file globals took its place
      (Item 3 phases F/G, § 13)
- [x] Smoke test every feature — per-phase, `docs/SMOKE_TESTS.md`
- [x] Deploy to production domain — 2026-05-02, `https://procabinet.app`

### Optional / stretch

- [x] Add Vite (build step, HMR) — 2026-04-30 (Item 3 phases A/B/D)
- [x] Supabase row types + JSDoc type-checking — full `strict: true` across
      all src files by 2026-05-02 (Item 3 phases F/G)
- [x] Move logo from base64 to Supabase Storage — `business-assets/` bucket,
      2026-04-28 (base64 localStorage copy kept as legacy fallback)
- [x] Unify Cabinet Builder + Cabinet Quote — post-launch, 2026-05-03 → 05-05
      (Item 2; `cq*` → `cb*` rename 2026-05-02)

### Explicitly deferred

- Tests — still deferred; `npm run typecheck` is the only automated gate
- Performance optimization — picked up 2026-06-11 once boot size mattered
  (boot bundle 1.24 MB → 652 KB; § 13)
- Real-time collaboration — still deferred; Supabase realtime is used for
  live-link status sync since 2026-06-09, which is not collaboration

---

## 7. Success criteria

The refactor is done when **all of these are true** (re-verified 2026-06-11):

- [x] `grep -r "localStorage.setItem" src/` returns only UI-pref keys — *with
      known exceptions*: the deliberate dual-write / legacy-fallback net still
      writes `pc_cl_pieces`/`pc_cl_sheets` (`_saveCutList`),
      `pc_order_prodstarts`, `pc_stock_libraries`, and `pc_biz_logo`.
      Postgres is the source of truth; these are write-only safety copies
- [x] `index.html` contains no inline `<script>` block — as shipped it's one
      `<script type="module">` bridge + ~40 `<script defer src="/src/*.js">`
      classic tags (deliberate deviation from "ES modules only", § 13
      2026-04-30)
- [x] `index.html` contains no `<style>` block (only `<link rel="stylesheet">`)
- [ ] ~~No single source file exceeds 1500 lines~~ — **not met, consciously
      relaxed**: `cutlist.js` 5,167 · `app.js` 2,194 · `quotes.js` 1,848 ·
      `cabinet.js` 1,825 (counts 2026-06-11; remaining files are under)
- [x] Manual smoke test passes (see § 11)
- [x] A fresh browser (incognito) can sign up, create a client, project, cut
      list, edge band, quote, and order — and refreshing preserves everything
      (in production use since 2026-05-02, including real customer signups)
- [x] Opening the app on a second device shows the same data — DB-backed,
      verified in daily cross-device use
- [x] At least one cross-project SQL query runs successfully — verified
      2026-06-11: `quotes × quote_lines` per-status aggregate with distinct
      client counts runs in Supabase SQL
- [x] Production deploy is reachable at the public URL with HTTPS —
      `https://procabinet.app` since 2026-05-02

---

## 8. Failure modes

What could go wrong, and how you'd know:

| Failure mode | Signal | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Scope creep — refactor becomes a rewrite | More than 2× over time budget | Re-read § 4; cut features |
| Data loss migrating localStorage to DB | Smoke test reveals missing data | Export-to-JSON tool first; keep localStorage as fallback for one release |
| Module split breaks inline handlers silently | Buttons do nothing in production | Smoke test every clickable element; grep `onclick=` and verify each function is on `window` |
| State migration introduces stale-reference bugs | UI shows old data after edits | Audit reads of mutated state; rely on render-after-write pattern |
| Half-done state — half migrated, app inconsistent | App works in dev, breaks under real use | Land each phase as its own commit; never merge a half-finished phase |
| Hidden cross-feature coupling discovered mid-refactor | Module A fails because of Module B | Keep `app.js` checkpoint commit so you can bail to single-file if needed |
| Vite setup eats a day | Build won't deploy | Time-box Vite to 4 hours; if not working, defer |
| Burnout / abandonment | You stop after phase 1 | Front-load DB normalization (the irreversible one); accept that "modules later" is a valid stop |
| Schema design has gaps revealed by code | Need to add columns mid-build | Keep migrations additive; never destructive until every feature uses the new shape |
| Logo / image data too large for jsonb | Insert fails or quota errors | Move to Supabase Storage from day one |

> *(None of these materialized as launch blockers. The closest calls: the
> dual-write safety net was kept rather than removed — see § 7 — and schema
> gaps did surface post-launch, handled as additive migrations per the
> mitigation, e.g. the `order_lines` parity fix, § 13 2026-06-10.)*

---

## 9. Open questions (resolve before starting)

All resolved — outcomes below, details in § 13 under the dates given.

- [x] **Cabinet systems**: deferred at refactor time (2026-04-28), then
      unified post-launch as Item 2 (2026-05-03 → 05-05); `cq*` → `cb*`
      rename 2026-05-02
- [x] **Catalog storage**: ~~Per-user tables (`materials_catalog`) or single
      jsonb column on `business_info`?~~ **Resolved** — single unified
      `catalog_items` table with a `type` column (`material` | `handle` |
      `finish` | `hardware`). Type-specific extras live in a `specs jsonb`
      field on the row. See `SCHEMA.md` § 3.2.
- [x] **Logo**: Supabase Storage — `business-assets/` bucket, URL on
      `business_info.logo_url` (2026-04-28); base64 copy kept as fallback
- [x] **Quote sources**: `cqSavedQuotes` dropped in the Phase 7 destructive
      cleanup (2026-04-29)
- [x] **Vite**: deferred 2026-04-28, reversed 2026-04-30 — in (dev server,
      build, env injection)
- [x] **Types**: JSDoc + `checkJs` under full `strict: true`, no `.ts` rename
      (Item 3 phases F/G, 2026-05-01 → 05-02)
- [x] **Migration approach**: phased per-feature, with DB + localStorage dual
      writes as the safety net (2026-04-28)
- [x] **Existing data**: exported — Phase 0 snapshot
      `Building Docs/snapshots/2026-04-28-prelaunch.json` + `_exportLocal()`
- [x] **Smoke test list**: written — `docs/SMOKE_TESTS.md` (Phase 0,
      2026-04-28)

---

## 10. Phases

High-level only — granular task list goes in `PLAN.md` or a new `REFACTOR_PLAN.md`.

| # | Phase | Estimate | Description | Done |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 0 | Prep | ~2 hr | Export current localStorage to JSON. Snapshot the DB. Write the smoke test list. | ✅ 2026-04-28 |
| 1 | Schema | ~1 day | Apply migrations for new tables. RLS policies. Verify in Supabase SQL editor. | ✅ 2026-04-28 |
| 2 | Data migration code | ~1 day | Write `migrateLocalToDB()` one-shot in current `index.html`. Run it; verify all data lands in tables. | ✅ 2026-04-28 |
| 3 | Code reads from DB | ~1 day | Replace localStorage reads with Supabase queries throughout. App still in one file. Smoke test. | ✅ 2026-04-28 |
| 4 | CSS extraction | ~1–2 hr | Pull all `<style>` blocks into `styles.css`. | ✅ 2026-04-28 |
| 5 | JS extraction | ~30 min | Pull `<script>` content to `src/app.js`. Verify. | ✅ 2026-04-28 |
| 6 | Module split | ~1 day | Split `app.js` into feature modules with imports/exports and `window.X` bindings. Smoke test. | ✅ 2026-05-01 — as a classic-script carve (Item 3 phase E), not ES modules |
| 7 | Cleanup | ~2 hr | Delete dead code surfaced by the split. | ✅ 2026-04-29 → 04-30 — destructive column cleanup + dead-code sweep |
| 8 | Optional | varies | Vite, types, etc. — only if Phases 1–7 stayed under budget. | ✅ 2026-04-30 → 05-02 — Vite + full strict types (Item 3) |
| 9 | Launch | varies | Production deploy. Real-domain click-through. Done. | ✅ 2026-05-02 — Cloudflare Pages cutover, `procabinet.app` |

> Each phase landed as its own commit(s), per the original rule.

---

## 11. Smoke test checklist

Written before Phase 1 as `docs/SMOKE_TESTS.md` and run per-phase; all passing
at the 2026-05-02 cutover. Superseded by daily production use since.

- [x] Sign up new user, sign in, sign out
- [x] Create / edit / delete a client
- [x] Create / edit / delete a project
- [x] Add stock items; edit category, supplier, variant
- [x] Cut list: add panels, add pieces, generate layout
- [x] Add edge bands; assign to piece sides
- [x] Cabinet Quote: add cabinet line, edit dimensions/materials, save quote
- [x] Convert quote to order
- [x] Update business info; upload logo; verify on PDF export
- [x] Export PDF, export CSV, import CSV
- [x] Toggle dark mode, change units, change currency
- [x] Refresh page → all data persists
- [x] Sign in on a second browser → same data appears

      cap; localStorage dual-write residue), annotated inline in § 7

---

## How to use this spec

This was the contract for the pre-launch refactor (written 2026-04-28, closed
out 2026-05-02). §§ 1–12 are kept as the historical record, annotated with
what actually shipped — including the deviations (classic-script carve instead
of ES modules, relaxed file-size cap, localStorage dual-write residue).

What stays live:

- **§ 13 (Decisions log)** — the ongoing project-wide log. One entry per
  non-obvious decision, oldest first. **Append new entries at the very end of
  this file** (per `CLAUDE.md`); § 13 is deliberately the last section so
  plain appends land in the right place.
- **`PLAN.md`** — current work, sub-steps, and status.

---

## 13. Decisions log

One entry per non-obvious decision — originally mid-refactor only, now the
ongoing project-wide log (per `CLAUDE.md`). Chronological, oldest first.
(Re-sorted and re-homed as the final section on 2026-06-11; five entries had
been stranded after the old closing section.)

- 2026-04-27 — **Catalog design**: unified `catalog_items` table with `type` column instead of separate `materials_catalog` / `handles_catalog` / `finishes_catalog` tables. Rationale: identical row shape across types; one place to manage prices; new categories become rows, not tables. See `SCHEMA.md` § 3.2.
- 2026-04-27 — **`SCHEMA.md` drafted** — full schema with DDL, RLS patterns, migration order. Marked Status: Draft pending review.
- 2026-04-28 — **Refactor scoped to Phases 0-3** (data layer only). Phases 4-7 (CSS/JS extraction, module split, destructive migrations, deploy) deferred to a follow-up refactor session, with prototyping in between. Plan at `~/.claude/plans/lets-plan-the-refactor-wobbly-lighthouse.md`.
- 2026-04-28 — **Vite deferred** — vanilla ES modules with no build step remain the target for the eventual module split.
- 2026-04-28 — **Cabinet systems unification deferred** to post-launch. `cqLines` migrates to `quote_lines`; `cabItems` migrates to `cabinet_templates`. Both subsystems coexist during refactor.
- 2026-04-28 — **Logo storage**: Supabase Storage bucket `business-assets/`, URL on `business_info.logo_url`. Replaces base64 in `pc_biz_logo`.
- 2026-04-28 — **Migration approach**: phased per-feature (not big-bang). Dual writes (DB + localStorage) maintained through Phase 3 and during prototyping pause as safety net.
- 2026-04-28 — **Orphan localStorage keys resolved**: `pc_stock_libraries` dropped (no migration target — `stock_items` is source of truth); `pc_order_prodstarts` → new `orders.production_start_date` column; `pc_cq_settings` rates → new columns on `business_info`; `pc_cq_projects` → migrate to `projects` + `quote_lines` rows.
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 0 (Prep) complete**: `docs/SMOKE_TESTS.md` created at project root; Supabase JSON snapshot at `Building Docs/snapshots/2026-04-28-prelaunch.json` (28 rows across 5 tables); `_exportLocal()` button added to Settings panel (`index.html` lines 1233-1241, function at line 3028).
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 1 (Schema additive) complete**: 9 migrations applied to Supabase project `mhzneruvlfmhnsohfrdo`. Created 11 new tables (`business_info`, `catalog_items`, `cabinet_templates`, `cabinets`, `cabinet_hardware`, `sheets`, `edge_bands`, `pieces`, `piece_edges`, `quote_lines`, `order_lines`); added 9 columns to `stock_items`, 4 to `orders`, 2 to `quotes`. All new tables have RLS enabled with full owner CRUD policies (4 policies each), except `piece_edges` which uses chained-ownership Pattern B (1 ALL policy). All 28 existing rows across the original 5 tables verified intact post-migration. No security advisor warnings related to the new schema.
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 1.5 (Unify project-save) complete**: new `_saveProjectScoped({ name, scope, payload })` at `index.html` line 8087 ensures one canonical `projects` row per `(user_id, name)`. Both `_clSaveProjectByName` (line 8119) and `cqSaveProject` (line 9039) now call it — Cut List with `scope: 'cutlist'`, Cabinet Quote with `scope: 'quote'`. Scope payload is merged into `projects.data` jsonb under `data.cutlist` / `data.quote` for now (Phase 3 will switch to writing into child tables). cqSaveProject still ALSO writes to `pc_cq_projects` localStorage for backward compatibility through the prototyping window.
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 2 (Migration) complete**: Storage bucket `business-assets` created (public, 512KB max, image MIME types only) with owner-folder RLS policies on `storage.objects`. New `migrateLocalToDB()` orchestrator at `index.html` line 3475 runs 9 idempotent subroutines: `_migrateBizInfo`, `_migrateCatalog`, `_migrateStock`, `_migrateCabinets`, `_migrateCutListProjects`, `_migrateCQProjects`, `_migrateSavedQuotes`, `_migrateOrderRefs`, `_dropStockLibraries`. Idempotency via tag-based notes (`[CQMIG:id]`, `[SAVEDMIG:id]`) on `quotes` and check-then-insert pattern on `catalog_items` / `cabinet_templates`. Logo upload migrates `pc_biz_logo` base64 → Supabase Storage `business-assets/{user_id}/logo.{ext}`. UI: "Run Migration to Database" button in Settings → Backup & Migration; results shown in `_showMigrationLog()` modal with summary line and per-subroutine status. JS parses cleanly (519KB, 12,030 lines total).
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 3 (all 8 features) complete** with **fallback-safe pattern**: each helper checks DB column / array first, falls back to localStorage if empty. Safe to land before/regardless of when migration runs. Done: **3.1 Stock metadata** — `_scGet/_ssGet/_svGet` prefer `stockItems[i].category/supplier/...` over localStorage maps; setters dual-write via new `_stockUpdateCols(id, updates, lsKey, lsValue)` helper. **3.2 Catalogs** — `loadAllData` extended to load `catalog_items` and `business_info` in parallel; new `_applyCatalogFromDB(rows)` overlays material/handle/finish arrays onto `cabSettings`/`cqSettings`. **3.3 Business info** — `_applyBizInfoFromDB(rows)` updates form inputs and rate defaults from DB; `saveBizInfo` now triggers debounced `_syncBizInfoToDB(payload)` (800ms); `handleLogoUpload` uploads to Storage `business-assets/{user_id}/logo.{ext}` and writes URL to `business_info.logo_url`. **3.4 Cabinets** — new `_loadCabItemsFromDB()` overlays `cabinet_templates` rows into `cabItems` on auth; `saveCabItems` triggers debounced `_syncCabItemsToDB()` (800ms) which INSERTs new and UPDATEs existing (tracked by `cab.db_id` field); `removeCabinetItem` also DELETEs the corresponding `cabinet_templates` row. **3.5 Cut list** — `loadProject(id)` queries `sheets`/`pieces`/`edge_bands` tables for the project; falls back to `projects.data` jsonb if DB child rows are empty; `_saveProjectScoped` for `scope: 'cutlist'` now calls `_replaceCutListChildTables(projectId, payload)` (REPLACE semantics). `_clSaveProjectByName` payload extended to include `edgeBands`. **3.6 Cabinet Quote** — `_saveProjectScoped` for `scope: 'quote'` calls `_replaceQuoteLinesChildTable(projectId, payload)`; finds-or-creates a tagged `[CQ_DEFAULT]` quote per project, deletes old `quote_lines` and inserts current `cqLines` via shared `_cqLineToRow()` helper. **3.7 Quotes UI** — Quote popup now has a "Quote Number" input (`pq-quote-number`); `_saveQuotePopup` writes `quote_number` to the `quotes` table. **3.8 Order helpers** — `_oqGet/_oqSet`, `_onGet/_onSet`, `setOrderProdStart`, `_restoreProdStarts` all prefer `orders.quote_id`/`notes`/`production_start_date` columns; setters dual-write to DB. JS parses cleanly throughout.
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 4 (CSS extraction) complete**: 1,125-line stylesheet extracted from `index.html` `<style>` block to `styles.css`. HTML now references via `<link rel="stylesheet" href="styles.css">`. Five other `<style>` tags in the file are intentionally left in place — they live inside JS template literals for PDF/print output, not part of the page CSS.
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 5 (JS extraction) complete**: entire `<script>` block (10,500+ lines) extracted from `index.html` to `src/app.js`. HTML now references via `<script src="src/app.js"></script>`. `index.html` shrunk from 12,467 → 798 lines (pure HTML markup). `src/app.js` parses cleanly.
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 6 (PARTIAL — module split): migrate code extracted to `src/migrate.js`**. The 489-line migration block (`_migReadLS`, `_migLog`, 9 subroutines, `migrateLocalToDB`, `_runMigration`, `_showMigrationLog`, `_cqLineToRow`) was lifted out of `app.js` and loaded via a second classic `<script>` tag after `app.js`. Both files share the global namespace, so no `window.X` exports needed for inline handlers. **Deeper ES-module split deferred** — switching to `<script type="module">` would require explicit `window.X = X` for ~80–100 functions called from 369 inline event handlers, plus per-feature state-object refactor; this is best done as a focused session with manual click-testing after each module is extracted. File state at end: `index.html` 798 lines · `styles.css` 1,126 lines · `src/app.js` 10,057 lines · `src/migrate.js` 494 lines.
- 2026-04-28 — **Phase 7 (destructive migrations) deferred**: dropping legacy columns (`quotes.client/project/materials/labour`, `orders.client/project/value`) and renaming `projects.data → ui_prefs` requires that no code path still reads them. Today the Quote popup still writes/reads `materials` and `labour` (the legacy totals fields), and the legacy text columns are still used as fallbacks where `client_id`/`project_id` FKs are null. Deferred until: (a) Quote totals are derived from `quote_lines` aggregation, and (b) all `client`/`project` text fallbacks are replaced with FK lookups.
- 2026-04-29 — **Phase 7 (destructive cleanup) complete**, in seven committed steps. (1) Added FK-resolving helpers `quoteClient/quoteProject/orderClient/orderProject` and a `quoteTotalsFromLines` aggregator that fills `q._totals = {materials, labour}` for every quote on load; `quoteTotal()` reads the cache. (2) Mechanical perl swap of every bare `q.client`/`q.project`/`o.client`/`o.project` for the helpers across `src/app.js`, plus dropping the same keys from row inserts in `convertQuoteToOrder`, `_saveQuotePopup`, `_saveOrderPopup`, `createQuote`, `duplicateQuote`, `duplicateOrder`, the CSV importers, and migrate.js. (3) Manual-totals quote UX writes a single `quote_lines` row (`name='Manual Quote'`, `material_cost_override` + `labour_hours` + `labour_override=true`); the popup's per-quote "Rate /hr" input is gone — labour now uses the global `cqSettings.labourRate`. Backfilled all 12 surviving quotes via `_writeManualTotalsLine(q.id, materials, labour/rate)`. (4) `convertQuoteToOrder` copies `quote_lines → order_lines`; `duplicateOrder` does the same. (5) `_saveProjectScoped` no longer merges scope payloads into the projects row — child tables (sheets/pieces/edge_bands/quote_lines) are the source of truth; `loadProject`'s `else { /* legacy data jsonb */ }` block deleted. (6) Snapshot saved at `Building Docs/snapshots/2026-04-29-pre-phase7.json`; orphan rows deleted (11 quotes + 3 orders, all with NULL FKs and prototyping garbage like "njcncsd"/"sdcsdv"); destructive migrations applied in three commits (`phase7_quotes_drop_legacy_columns`, `phase7_orders_drop_legacy_text_columns`, `phase7_projects_rename_data_to_ui_prefs`). (7) Status flipped above. **Deviation from SCHEMA.md § 3.15:** kept `orders.value`. Reason: `order_lines` aggregation produces materials+labour only; the customer-paid total snapshotted at quote→order conversion includes markup+tax that cannot be reconstructed from lines alone (orders have no markup/tax columns and the parent quote may be edited or deleted later). Adding markup/tax to orders was out of scope. The plain-English schema doc and code comment in `orderTotal()` flag this.

- 2026-04-30 — **Item 3 phases A/B/D landed** (Vite scaffold + npm deps + TS toolchain), reversing the earlier 2026-04-28 Vite-deferred decision. (A) `package.json` + `vite.config.mjs` add Vite as dev server (`npm run dev`, port 3000) and build tool (`npm run build` → `dist/`). A `copy-classic-scripts` plugin in vite config copies `src/*.js` into `dist/src/` so the existing classic `<script src="src/*.js">` tags resolve from the build output without any source-file changes. `.claude/launch.json` adds a "Vite dev" config alongside the existing npx-serve config. (B) Replaced the three CDN `<script>` tags (`@supabase/supabase-js`, `jspdf`, `jspdf-autotable`) with npm packages bundled by Vite. The actual swap uses a tiny module bridge (`src/main.js`) that imports the npm packages and re-exposes them on `window` under the same names the CDN scripts provided (`window.supabase.createClient`, `window.jspdf.jsPDF`); this lets `db.js`/`app.js`/`migrate.js` stay as classic scripts unchanged. The four classic source `<script>` tags got `defer` added so they execute after the deferred-by-default module bridge sets up the globals. (D) Added `typescript` + `@types/node` devDeps and a permissive `tsconfig.json` (`allowJs:true`, `checkJs:false`, `strict:false`, `noEmit:true`); `npm run typecheck` passes clean. **Deviated from plan #3:** skipped what the plan called phase C (bulk `<script type="module">` swap with a 150-name window-shim) — the bridge module already lets npm packages flow into classic source files, so the bulk conversion brings little value before phase E (module split) actually needs it. Phase E will introduce ESM into source files incrementally as functions get carved out, rather than as a big-bang conversion. Phases E (module split, 8–12 commits), F (`.ts` everywhere), G (strict mode + DB types), and H (deploy cutover) remain TODO.

- 2026-05-01 — **Item 3 phase F partial** (15/19 src files type-checked, 7 commits). Phase F kicks off the TypeScript-coverage push. **Deviated from plan #3**: the plan said "rename *.js → *.ts and add @ts-nocheck", but the codebase is classic-script-loaded (each src/*.js gets its own `<script defer>` tag, not ES modules), so a bulk rename would break dev/build until Vite is taught to compile .ts back to classic-loadable .js. Instead, took the pragmatic first step: enabled `checkJs: true` in `tsconfig.json` and added `// @ts-nocheck` to every src/*.js, then started peeling per-file. Files .js stay as-is; type-checking happens via JSDoc + a new `src/globals.d.ts` ambient-declarations file (Window stash slots for inline-handler render state, the npm-bridge globals from main.js). Files now type-checking clean (no `@ts-nocheck`): `main.js`, `backup.js`, `db.js`, `ui.js`, `forms.js`, `auth.js`, `business.js`, `schedule.js`, `settings.js`, `orders.js`, `projects.js`, `dashboard.js`, `migrate.js`, `clients.js`, `app.js`. Common patterns introduced: per-file `_xInput(id)` helpers casting `getElementById` to `HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement | HTMLSelectElement`; `+date` coercion for `isNaN(Date)` / `Date - Date`; `String(...)` coercion for `.textContent =` and `localStorage.setItem(...)` numeric values; `/** @type {HTMLImageElement|HTMLCanvasElement|HTMLButtonElement} */` casts where elements have specific properties (`src` / `width` / `disabled` / etc.). One key cross-cutting fix: `src/db.js`'s `_DBBuilder.then()` got a JSDoc `@returns {Promise<...>}` so every `await _db(...)` chain elsewhere typechecks; the `return this` line is `// @ts-expect-error`'d because the builder is structurally a fake-thenable that recurses (it returns `this`, not a real Promise, but `this` is itself thenable). Files **still carrying `@ts-nocheck`**: `stock.js` (745 lines, 75 errors), `quotes.js` (872, 37 errors), `cabinet.js` (2,296), `cutlist.js` (2,805) — all the big domain files. Each has dozens of identical-shape `.value`-on-`HTMLElement` errors scattered across many functions; grinding them one-by-one is a poor effort/value match. They're deferred to a future session, possibly with a sed-replace pass once the `_xInput`-helper pattern is consistent across all already-peeled files. Phase F's plan-3 step "rename *.js → *.ts" remains future work — meaningful only after the remaining big files have peeled their nocheck or once Vite gets a build pipeline that compiles `.ts` for classic-script tags.

Smaller functions used inline JSDoc casts (3 onclick assignments in cabinet.js's `_clLoadCabinetParts` merge popup; 4 `_byId(targetInputId).value = name` sites in quotes.js). One additional `if (!el) return;` early guard added to `renderStockMain` (line 636 — covers 100+ uses of `el` in the function body). **Patterns NOT introduced**: still no globals.d.ts changes (sub-G.2's job); no _byId signature change beyond nullability (subtype lie kept until the codebase decides whether per-call-site `HTMLButtonElement | HTMLImageElement | etc.` discrimination is worth the diff cost); no silent-fallback runtime behavior changes. **End-state**: tsconfig has `strictNullChecks: true`, other strict knobs unchanged. `npm run typecheck` clean. `npm run build` produces working dist/. Comprehensive smoke verified: reload + 8 nav tabs (dashboard/stock/cabinet/quote/orders/schedule/clients/cutlist) all panel-active, demo data persists (1 sheet, 5 pieces), cutlist `optimize()` runs and produces 3 canvases with non-empty results-area, no console errors. Sub-pass B alone: 6 commits across 4 files (cutlist counted twice — once for non-_byId fixes in B.2, once for _byId in B.3 alongside the ui.js narrow; quotes/cabinet/stock once each). Cumulative G.1 push: 17 commits, ~480 errors fixed. Phase G.2 (tighten globals.d.ts Element/EventTarget augs), G.3 (`noImplicitAny: true`), and G.4 (Supabase row types via `generate_typescript_types` MCP + `_DBBuilder<T>` wiring) remain future work — separate plans.
- 2026-05-02 — **Item 3 phase G.4 complete — Supabase row types + `_DBBuilder<K, Single>` generic** (1 commit). G.4 was promoted ahead of G.2/G.3 in the same session because it has the highest bug-finding value of the three remaining strict sub-phases. Generated `src/database.types.ts` via the Supabase MCP `generate_typescript_types` tool against project `mhzneruvlfmhnsohfrdo` — 16 tables (`business_info`, `cabinet_hardware`, `cabinet_templates`, `cabinets`, `catalog_items`, `clients`, `edge_bands`, `order_lines`, `orders`, `piece_edges`, `pieces`, `projects`, `quote_lines`, `quotes`, `sheets`, `stock_items`) plus the standard `Tables<T>` / `TablesInsert<T>` / `TablesUpdate<T>` helpers. The generated file is committed as-is so types are reproducible without an MCP round-trip; regenerate after schema migrations. **`_DBBuilder` rewritten as `_DBBuilder<K extends _TableName, Single extends boolean = false>`**: every chainable method (`select` / `insert` / `update` / `delete` / `eq` / `order` / `limit`) preserves both K and Single; `.single()` flips Single to true. The `.then()` resolver type uses a conditional — `{data: Single extends true ? Row | null : Row[] | null}` — so callers get the right shape based on what builder methods they chained. `_db()` is generic on K so `_db('clients').select()` returns `Promise<{data: Tables<'clients'>[] | null}>`. `eq` / `order`'s `col` parameter typed as `keyof Row` so column-name typos error out. `update` body typed as `Tables[K]['Update']`, `insert` body as `Insert | Insert[]`. The fake-thenable `return this` pattern is preserved (still uses `@ts-expect-error`); the conditional-return-type narrowing inside the `.then` handler casts through `any` at the resolve site since generic-conditional-narrowing-inside-handler is a TS limitation. **Schema-divergence bugs surfaced and TODO'd** (NOT fixed in this commit — they're behavior-affecting and need their own audit): `stock.js addStockItem`'s in-memory `data.thickness/width/length` shadow the DB columns `thickness_mm/width_mm/length_m` (desync after page reload); `quotes.js _openNewClientPopup` / `_openNewProjectPopup` pass `id: Date.now()` to Supabase Insert (the DB has serial id and silently overrides; the local `newProject` also has extra `client/desc/status` fields not in the projects schema); `app.js`'s update-project popup writes `status` and `description` columns that don't exist on `projects`; `app.js loadAllData` adds an in-memory `status: 'active'` to project rows. All four cast through `any` with TODO(schema-divergence) comments. Mechanical fixes (no behavior change): `.single()` callers got `if (error || !data) return;` null guards (data is now `Row | null`, was `any`); `delete nl.id` / `delete nl.quote_id` patterns in orders/quotes cast through `any` (delete operator forbids non-optional fields under strict); `ui_prefs` Json access in projects.js + migrate.js cast through `any`; `cabinet_templates.default_specs` Json spread cast. Verified: typecheck clean across all 19 src files; reload + 8 nav tabs render; demo data persists; cutlist `optimize()` produces 3 canvases; no console errors.
- 2026-05-02 — **Item 3 phase G.2 complete — globals.d.ts Element/EventTarget tightening** (1 commit). The Phase F transition augmentations on `Element` + `EventTarget` (value, style, focus, select, dataset, src, width, height, getContext, toDataURL, files, checked, disabled, closest, placeholder etc.) were a hack to let peeled .js files avoid per-call casts; with G.1 (strictNullChecks) and G.4 (DB types) in, those properties belong on the proper subtypes. Removed the entire augs block from `src/globals.d.ts` (kept the Window-stash-slots block — those are legitimate cross-file globals + npm-bridge globals). **Surprisingly small cascade**: 17 errors total across cabinet.js (4), cutlist.js (10), quotes.js (3) — all `querySelector` / `querySelectorAll` call sites that didn't narrow. Standard fix pattern adopted: cast the iterator type, not each call site. `/** @type {NodeListOf<HTMLElement>} */ (qSAll(...)).forEach(...)` applied once and the forEach callback gets `b: HTMLElement` for free (used 9 times across the three files). For single-element results: cast inline (`/** @type {HTMLElement | null} */ (qS(...))`) — used twice in cutlist for `.cl-left` and the table-cell focus target. Specific subtypes for narrower types: `NodeListOf<HTMLCanvasElement>` for canvas spread→toDataURL; `HTMLInputElement | null` for the input that receives focus+select. Plus an ad-hoc `Array.from(sidebar.children).filter(...)` cast to `HTMLElement[]` once for the cabinet builder/rates tab toggle. The Window declarations block in globals.d.ts is untouched. Verified: typecheck clean; reload + cutlist optimize() → 3 canvases; toggleCol('grain') and toggleEdgeBandCol() execute without console errors (those were among the rewired call sites).
- 2026-05-02 — **Item 3 phase G.3 complete — noImplicitAny + full strict mode** (10 commits, ~1260 errors fixed across all 17 non-clean src files). Closed out the strict-mode push: tsconfig now has `strict: true` (which expands to `noImplicitAny + strictNullChecks + useUnknownInCatchVariables + strictFunctionTypes + alwaysStrict + strictPropertyInitialization + noImplicitThis + strictBindCallApply`). All 19 src files type-check clean. **Initial flag flip**: 1247 errors total — 627 TS7006 (untyped params), 480 TS7005/7034 (untyped vars/declarators including cross-file `let` globals), 53 TS7053 (untyped object indexing), plus a few others. **G.3.1 (cross-file global annotations, 1 commit, ~290 errors closed)**: each src/*.js file's top-level `let`-declared global got a JSDoc type annotation right at the declaration site — `_userId: string | null`, `orders: Tables<'orders'>[]`, `quotes: Tables<'quotes'>[]`, `stockItems: Tables<'stock_items'>[]`, `clients: Tables<'clients'>[]`, `projects: (Tables<'projects'> & {status?: string})[]`, plus `any[]` for the in-memory cut-list/cabinet-quote state (sheets / pieces / edgeBands / cqLines / cqLibrary / etc.). Source-side annotation chosen over `globals.d.ts` `var` declarations because TS treats classic-script files as scripts (not modules) and `var` in a d.ts conflicts with `let` in source under TS2451 redeclare. **G.3.2 (per-file annotation, 9 commits, ~970 errors closed)**: smallest-first attack order — auth/forms/ui/settings/business/schedule/orders cleared in batches of 1-30 errors each, then projects/dashboard/clients/migrate/app/quotes/stock/cabinet/cutlist as the larger files. Patterns adopted: `/** @param {string} foo */` JSDoc above every untyped function (mostly mechanical `string`/`number`/`any` annotations); `/** @type {Record<string, T>} */` on lookup-table object literals (STATUS_LABELS, GRAIN_ICONS, CL_COLS, statusColMap, etc.) so dynamic-key indexing works; `i.qty ?? 0` / `o.value ?? 0` / `q.markup ?? 0` everywhere arithmetic uses nullable schema columns; row-literal cast-through-any at insert/update boundaries where the local in-memory shape has fields beyond the DB schema. The `cqSettings` declaration in cabinet.js cast `any` because the codebase mutates it dynamically (adds edgeBanding sub-keys, labourTimes, materials lists, etc.) — stricter typing would force a giant union. For the deepest nested callbacks (drawCanvas's buildGuillotinePlan + 30+ inner arrow callbacks in cutlist.js), a small Python script auto-injected JSDoc by parsing the typecheck output and inserting `/** @param {any} name */ (name) =>` rewrites; verified by re-running typecheck. **G.3.3 (final commit + strict:true)**: flipped `strict: true` in tsconfig as a sanity check — surfaced exactly 13 TS18046 errors, all `useUnknownInCatchVariables` (catch `e` is `unknown` instead of `any`). All same shape: `(/** @type {any} */ (e)).message || e` cast at the access site, batch-fixed with another small Python script. Other strict flags (`strictFunctionTypes`, `strictPropertyInitialization`, `noImplicitThis`, `strictBindCallApply`) surfaced zero new errors — the codebase was already conformant. **Anti-patterns avoided**: no `// @ts-nocheck` reintroductions; no silent runtime changes (every `??` substitution preserves the original `||` semantics where the field is nullable; the `any` casts at row boundaries match what the runtime already does). Verified: `npm run typecheck` clean under full `strict: true`; reload + 8 nav tabs render; demo data persists; cutlist optimize() runs without errors; no console errors. Phase G is now closed in full — tsconfig is strict, DB row types thread through `_DBBuilder<K, Single>`, and the Element/EventTarget augs are gone. Plan-3's remaining items (rename `*.js` → `*.ts`, deploy cutover) are independent of strict mode and tracked separately.
- 2026-05-02 — **Phase H1 follow-up — GitHub Actions auto-deploy wired** (1 workflow file, 2 commits + 1 SPEC commit). After confirming Cloudflare's dashboard doesn't allow converting a direct-upload Pages project to git-connected (Settings exposes only Variables/Bindings/Runtime/General — no Source/Builds-and-deployments tab on direct-upload projects), pivoted to GitHub Actions. New `.github/workflows/deploy.yml` runs on push to `main` and on `workflow_dispatch`: checkout → setup-node@v4 (Node 20) → `npm ci` → `npm run typecheck` (gate) → `npm run build` (with VITE_SUPABASE_URL + VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY hardcoded inline — they're publishable values, already in every deployed bundle, so not actually secrets) → `cloudflare/wrangler-action@v3` deploys `dist/` to the cabinetry-app project. Two repo secrets used: `CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN` (custom token scoped to Account / Cloudflare Pages / Edit, restricted to user's account) and `CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID` (`cf6a335f2b8b6fded3b921c9e318ba03`). **First run validation**: pushed all 100 unpushed local commits + the new workflow → workflow ran in 40s end-to-end → all steps green → procabinet.app served the same bundle hash (deterministic build). **Subtle gotchas hit and resolved**: (a) `gh push` rejected with `OAuth App ... without 'workflow' scope`; gh's default scopes are `gist, read:org, repo`, so `gh auth refresh -s workflow` was required to add the scope. (b) Local branch was 100+ commits ahead of remote (the entire Phase E/F/G/H sequence had been worked locally without pushing) and remote had 1 ahead (`Delete CNAME`, auto-committed by GitHub when the custom domain was removed from Pages settings); first attempted `git pull --rebase` half-applied 50 of 100 commits before failing on a working-tree-overwrite conflict in db.js/ui.js; recovered with `git rebase --abort` (which re-popped the autostash automatically) then `git merge origin/main --no-edit` for a clean merge commit. (c) macOS iCloud sync produced ~25 untracked `* 2.*` duplicate files in the working tree; left untracked, ignored. **Heads-up logged**: GitHub annotation warns Node 20 actions deprecate June 2026; bump to Node 24 / actions@v5 ahead of that date. Local-dev escape hatch (manual `npm run build && npx wrangler pages deploy dist --project-name=cabinetry-app --branch=main`) still works for emergencies.

- 2026-05-02 — **Schema-divergence H0.3 — quotes popup inserts: Date.now() ids dropped, schema-mismatch fields removed** (1 commit, addresses bug #2 from G.4's TODO audit). Both popup-creation flows in `quotes.js` were creating in-memory rows with `id: Date.now()`, pushing optimistically, then firing-and-forgetting an insert. The DB has serial PKs that silently override; the in-memory array ended up with phantom Date.now() ids that didn't match the DB rows — every subsequent `.find(p => p.id === ...)` mismatched. **`_saveNewClientPopup`**: drops `id: Date.now()`, awaits `_db('clients').insert(insertBody).select().single()`, errors-and-returns on failure (toast + console.error), pushes the DB-returned `data` (with the real serial id). Pattern matches `stock.js:523` already-correct insert flow. **`_saveNewProjectPopup`**: same pattern, plus drops the schema-mismatch fields — `client: clientName` (string) is replaced by `client_id: cli?.id ?? null` via a `clients.find(c => c.name === clientName)` lookup; `desc` becomes `description` (the H0.1 column); the Insert type is now `Tables<'projects'>['Insert']`-compatible without the `/** @type {any} */` cast. **`_autoFillClientFromProject` rewritten** (the only consumer of the legacy `proj.client` shadow string): now reads `proj.client_id`, looks up the matching client in the `clients` array, fills the input with `cli.name`. This fixes a latent bug — projects loaded from the DB previously had no `client` shadow field, so the autofill silently failed for every existing project; now it works for both newly-created and DB-loaded projects. **All 5 TODO(schema-divergence) sites from G.4 are now resolved.** **Verification**: `npm run typecheck` clean; `npm run build` clean; reload console clean; preview eval probe injected a fake project (`client_id: 888`) + matching client (`id: 888, name: "Probe Client"`) and confirmed `_autoFillClientFromProject` correctly resolved and filled `"Probe Client"`. End-to-end UI smoke deferred — preview unauthenticated this session.
- 2026-05-02 — **Schema-divergence H0.2 — stock_items shadow field hydration on load** (1 commit, addresses bug #1 from G.4's TODO audit). The codebase pervasively reads stock-item edge-band metadata via short shadow names (`thickness`/`width`/`length`/`glue`) in cut-list dropdowns and edge-band UI; the DB columns added in Phase 7 are `thickness_mm`/`width_mm`/`length_m`/`glue`. Insert-time path at `stock.js:528-535` set the shadow fields directly on the post-insert row, so they were correct for the immediate session but lost after reload — `loadAllData` selected `*` from `stock_items` and the short names came back undefined. **Fix**: replaced `stockItems = stk || []` in `app.js loadAllData` with a load-time map that copies `thickness_mm → thickness`, `width_mm → width`, `length_m → length` whenever the source value is non-null. The `& { thickness?: number, width?: number, length?: number, thick?: number }` intersection on the `stockItems` declaration in `stock.js:303` already permits the shadow fields, so no type changes needed. The in-place mutations at `stock.js:530-535` stay (immediate-session correctness without waiting for reload); the TODO(schema-divergence) comment is replaced with a one-liner pointing at the load map. **Why not rename consumers**: the short names appear in template-literal HTML inside cut-list and edge-band code at ~30+ sites — separate rename pass, deferred. **Verification**: `npm run typecheck` clean; `npm run build` clean; reload console clean; SQL confirms 3 stock_items rows have the *_mm/*_m columns populated (id 20 Oak Veneer 2/22/50/Pre-glued is the canonical test case). UI smoke deferred — preview unauthenticated.

Closes Item 2; the Cabinet Builder ↔ Quote unification is fully shipped. **4.1 — catalog_items CRUD wiring**: new `_syncCatalogToDB()` in business.js — debounced 800ms REPLACE-semantics sync of `cbSettings.materials` / `cbSettings.hardware` / `cbSettings.finishes` to the `catalog_items` table (delete all rows for the user filtered to the three managed types, then re-insert from in-memory state). Wired into `saveCBSettings()` so inline edits in the My Rates panel persist past reload — fixes the prior bug where `_applyCatalogFromDB` re-applied stale rows after a TOKEN_REFRESHED. Race guard added to `_applyCatalogFromDB` (`if (_catalogSyncTimer) return`) matching the patterns from phase 1.5 / phase 3. `_DBBuilder` got a new `.in(col, vals)` method (PostgREST `column=in.(v1,v2,v3)` syntax) for the multi-type delete filter — kept the existing _DBBuilder shape, added one method. The 'handle' catalog type rows are not touched by the sync (cbSettings has no `handles` field after the cq→cb rename), so any rows of that type from old migrations are preserved. **4.2 — cbSavedQuotes removed**: state vars (`cbSavedQuotes`, `cbActiveQuoteIdx`), helpers (`loadCBSaved`, `saveCBSaved`), CRUD functions (`saveCBQuote`, `loadCBQuote`, `newCBQuote`, `deleteCBQuote`, `dupCBSavedQuote`), and the `renderCBSavedShelf` pill UI all deleted. The `pc_cq_saved` localStorage key is no longer written; `migrate.js _migrateSavedQuotes` still reads it for one-time legacy migration into the `quotes`/`quote_lines` tables. Init block at end of cabinet.js dropped the `loadCBSaved()` call. **4.3 — cbProjectLibrary removed**: state var, `loadCBProjectLibrary` / `saveCBProjectLibrary`, full CRUD (`cbSaveProject`, `cbLoadProject`, `cbDeleteProject`, `renderCBProjects`, `cbExportProjects`, `cbImportProjects`), and the `_cbSaveProjectByName` flow all deleted. `toggleCabPanel` simplified — used to handle 'projects' AND 'library' branches; now only the 'library' branch (cabinet template library, a separate concept). `pc_cq_projects` no longer written; `pc_cq_project_name` / `pc_cq_client_name` kept as nav-state pointers per the plan. Init block dropped the `loadCBProjectLibrary()` call. Migration helper still references `pc_cq_projects` for one-time read. **4.4 — converters slimmed (not dropped)**: discovered the plan's "drop entirely" framing was overstated. The converters (`_quoteLineRowToCB` / `_cbLineToRow`) ARE load-bearing, not dead weight: cb-only fields `backMat` / `doorMat` exist in the in-memory shape AND in renderCBEditor's UI inputs but have no matching schema columns (DB only stores `material`), so the round-trip silently collapses both back to the carcass material. Additionally, the full rename from camelCase → snake_case would touch ~250 cabinet.js sites and `.w` / `.h` / `.d` collide with `stockItems` (which has its own `w`/`h` columns) AND cutlist `pieces` (which has `p.w`/`p.h`). Slimmer outcome: kept the converter pair, added explicit `// ── cbLines ↔ quote_lines boundary converters ──` heading with a "Round-trip caveat" doc block listing the cb-only fields (`id`, `backMat`, `doorMat`) that don't survive a save → reload cycle, and a TODO note that the proper fix is `back_material` + `door_material` schema columns (deferred). The full rename is parked behind a future `cb*` → `qb*` symbol rename pass. **4.5 — file rename skipped**: `src/cabinet.js` → `src/quote-builder.js` rejected as a half-measure — the internal symbols still all start with `cb*` (`cbLines`, `cbSettings`, `calcCBLine`, `renderCBPanel`, etc.), and a 2,499-line pure-cosmetic git diff would muddy history without delivering enough mental-model gain on its own. Bundle with a future symbol-rename pass if it ever happens. **File deltas**: cabinet.js 2,705 → 2,499 lines (−206); business.js 164 → 199 lines (+35, the new sync helper); db.js +1 method (`.in()`). **Verification**: `npm run typecheck` clean; preview eval confirmed all 20 removed legacy symbols are now `undefined` and all 9 kept/new functions are `function`; reload + 4-tab smoke (cabinet/quote/stock/cutlist) all render; `toggleCabLibrary()` round-trips clean; no console errors. End-to-end DB-write verification of the catalog sync deferred — preview was unauthenticated this session, will smoke on procabinet.app.
- 2026-05-05 — **Item 2 phase 2 complete — UI unification**. Brings Cabinet Builder and Quotes onto one editing surface. **2.1 — project gate**: new `_ensureCBProject()` in cabinet.js auto-creates the `projects` row on first cabinet add when the typed name doesn't match an existing project (uses existing `resolveClient`/`resolveProject` from clients.js); `addCBLine` and `addCBLineFromPreset` are async and bail with a toast when no name is entered; new `_renderProjectStatus()` shows a "⚠ Select or create a project to save" hint under the project input when `_getCBProjectId()` returns null. **2.2 — Edit button**: new `editQuoteInCB(quoteId)` loads a quote's `quote_lines` via `_quoteLineRowToCB`, sets a new `cbEditingQuoteId` global (number = editing specific quote, null = editing project draft), persists to `localStorage('pc_cb_editing_quote_id')`, and switches to the cabinet tab. While set, `_syncCBLinesToDB()` routes through new `_syncCBLinesToQuote(id)` instead of the project draft — same delete-then-insert REPLACE semantics, plus `_refreshQuoteTotals(id)` so the quotes-tab `_totals` cache updates. `renderCBResults()` shows an "Editing: <project>" banner with Done/Discard buttons (replacing the normal-mode "Create Quote" button). `finishEditingQuote()` flushes the pending debounced sync and reloads the project draft via `_loadCBLinesFromDB()`. `discardQuoteEdits()` re-writes the snapshot in `cbEditingOriginalLines` to the DB before exiting. `_loadCBLinesFromDB()` extended to check the localStorage key and restore from the editing-quote's lines first, with an additional guard `if (cbEditingQuoteId && cbLines.length > 0) return` to prevent TOKEN_REFRESHED from clobbering an active edit. `removeQuote()` in quotes.js clears the editing localStorage when the deleted id matches. Edit button added to the quote-card footer in `renderQuoteMain`. **2.3 — Duplicate**: already shipped — the existing "Copy" button on quote cards calls `duplicateQuote(id)` (quotes.js:949), which already copies the quote row plus all `quote_lines` rows. No code change. **2.4 — Create Quote**: new `cbCreateQuoteFromDraft()` snapshots the current cbLines into a brand-new customer-facing quote (no `[CB_DRAFT]` tag) — calls `_ensureCBProject` for the project_id, builds a notes string from line specs, inserts the `quotes` row, then inserts the converted `quote_lines` via `_cbLineToRow`, then `_refreshQuoteTotals`. The draft stays as the live workspace, so the user can iterate and create additional quotes from the same project. Single "Create Quote" button replaces the old "Add to Existing Quote" / "+ New Quote" pair. Legacy `cbAddToNewQuote` / `cbAddToExistingQuote` kept as thin stubs that delegate to `cbCreateQuoteFromDraft()`; `_cbApplyToQuote` is a no-op stub. The legacy internals (form pre-fill, inline picker dropdown, append-to-existing path) were removed via an awk-based delete after the Edit tool struggled to match the unicode `×` / `—` characters in the source. **Verification**: `npm run typecheck` clean; preview eval confirmed all new functions defined, Edit button present on quote cards (`["Mark Sent","→ Order","Edit","Copy","Print","PDF"]`), normal-mode buttons (`["Create Quote","↓ PDF","⊕ Print","↓ Export","↑ Import"]`), editing-mode swaps to `["Done","Discard"]` with the banner shown, `cb-project-status` div in DOM. End-to-end DB-write smoke deferred — preview was unauthenticated this session.

- 2026-05-05 — **Door / drawer labour: per-count linear → m²/m³ power-law + multi-type**. Extended the carcass power-law to the rest of the labour model. New `cbSettings` arrays: `carcassTypes` / `doorTypes` / `drawerFrontTypes` / `drawerBoxTypes`, each with `{name, refHours}` rows; cabinet lines pick one type per category (`line.carcassType` / `doorType` / `drawerFrontType` / `drawerBoxType`). Power-law formulas `hours = refHours × (actual / reference)^0.7` use four hardcoded reference geometries derived from a 600×720×580 cabinet at 50% door / 30% drawer pct: `CARCASS_REF_VOLUME=0.25 m³`, `DOOR_REF_AREA=0.216 m²`, `DRAWER_FRONT_REF_AREA=0.1296 m²`, `DRAWER_BOX_REF_VOLUME=0.07517 m³` (constants in `src/cabinet-calc.js`). **Geometry semantic shift**: `doorPct` and `drawerPct` are now "% of full front face area" (silently reinterpreted from old "% of cabinet height"). New default `drawerPct=0`; door + drawer pcts clamp to ≤100 in the editor (`cbUpdatePct` helper in `src/cabinet.js` trims the partner pct), with an "Open: X%" readout under each slider. **Material formulas updated** to use `pct/100 × W × H` for total areas; drawer box height derived as `frontArea / drawers / innerW`. **Multi-type seeds**: Carcass:Standard / Doors:Slab+Shaker+Vinyl-Wrapped+Integrated Handle / Drawer Fronts:Slab+Shaker / Drawer Boxes:Standard+Dovetail (user can edit/delete). **DB**: migration `add_cb_labour_type_columns_to_business_info` adds 4 jsonb columns to `business_info` (`default_carcass_types`, `default_door_types`, `default_drawer_front_types`, `default_drawer_box_types`, all default `'[]'`). Regenerated `src/database.types.ts`. `_syncCBSettingsToDB` extended to upsert the 4 arrays; `_applyBizInfoFromDB` extended to overlay them on auth (only when DB row has non-empty arrays). **UI**: My Rates panel got 4 new collapsible "Types" sections (each with reference geometry in the title, e.g. "Door Types (per 0.22 m²)") and a renamed "Other Labour Times" section for the remaining fixed-rate components (Fixed Shelf, Adj. Holes, Loose Shelf, Partition, End Panel, Finish). Cabinet editor gained 4 type dropdowns (Carcass type in Cabinet section; Door type in Doors section; Front type + Box type in Drawers section). **Back-compat**: legacy `lt.door` / `lt.drawer` / `lt.carcass` fields ignored when type lists are present; old `doorPct=95` cabinets render visually similar under new semantics; no migration script needed.
- 2026-05-05 — **Carcass labour: linear → power-law scaling**. Replaced `autoLabour += (lt.carcass || 1.5) * volume` with `refHours × (volume / refVolume)^exponent` in both `calcCBLine` and `calcCBSections` (`src/cabinet-calc.js`). Three new `cbSettings.labourTimes` fields drive the curve: `carcassRefVolume` (default 0.25 m³ — typical 600×720×580 base cabinet), `carcassRefHours` (default 0.4 hrs), `carcassExponent` (default 0.7). Rationale: a cabinet twice as big does not take twice as long — most cabinet labour is surface work (cuts, banding, drilling, sanding), and surface area scales as V^(2/3) for similar shapes, so n in the 0.6-0.8 range matches reality. Old `lt.carcass: 1.5` field kept in defaults as a no-op for back-compat with persisted settings (the new fields take precedence). My Rates UI in `src/cabinet-render.js` swapped the single "Carcass (volume)" row for three rows ("Carcass: ref volume / ref hours / scaling (n)"). Calibration: at the reference volume the new formula yields exactly `refHours`; at 4× volume (1.0 m³) it yields ~1.06 hrs vs the old 1.5 hrs (linear) — large cabinets stop being penalized for size. No migration script needed; the legacy field is just ignored.

Same-day reversal of the multi-currency Stripe Prices decision: switched to USD-only ($35/mo, $299/yr) with Stripe Adaptive Pricing handling local-currency conversion at Checkout. UK Stripe account still settles in GBP via the FX spread. Migration `drop_business_info_preferred_currency` removed the column added earlier in the session — zero rows had non-null values, no code referenced it. Regenerated `database.types.ts`. **F.1 — limits module shipped**: new `src/limits.js` (loaded between `ui.js` and `orders.js` in index.html) declares `FREE_LIMITS` (frozen 5-each for clients/projects/quotes/orders/cabinet_templates/stock), `_subscription` global, `loadSubscription()`, `isPro()`, `getLimit()`, `isAtLimit()`, `isApproachingLimit()`. `loadAllData` kicks `loadSubscription()` off in parallel with the existing data fetches via `subPromise` (its return value isn't destructured — side effect updates the global). `signOut()` and the auth-state-change handler both reset `_subscription = null`. Returns false / cap=5 for everyone until S.6 webhook starts populating subscription rows. Docs updated: PLAN.md S.2/S.4/S.5/S.8 simplified for USD-only; PLAN.md F.1 marked done; SCHEMA.md § 3.1 reverted to original; SCHEMA.md § 3.17 (subscriptions) kept; § 5 modified-tables list cleaned. `npm run typecheck` clean.
- 2026-05-05 — **Stripe S.3 — subscriptions table + multi-currency prep**. Migration `create_subscriptions_and_preferred_currency` applied to project `mhzneruvlfmhnsohfrdo`. New `subscriptions` table tracks Pro state (`stripe_customer_id` unique-not-null, `stripe_subscription_id` unique, `stripe_price_id` cache for currency+cadence, `plan` text cache 'pro_monthly'/'pro_annual', `status`, `current_period_start/end`, `cancel_at_period_end`, `canceled_at`, timestamps). Free users have **no row** — null/missing = free. RLS deviates from Pattern A: SELECT-only policy for `user_id = auth.uid()`; no INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE policies (Stripe webhooks write via service role, bypassing RLS). Prevents users from forging subscription rows for themselves. - 2026-05-06 — **Multi-unit format system** (new file `src/units.js`, ~10 files changed, 1 DB migration). Added `formatDim()` / `parseDim()` / `convertDim()` / `unitLabel()` in a new `src/units.js` loaded before `cutlist.js`. `window.unitFormat = { mode, decimals, denominator }` alongside existing `window.units`. Imperial modes: decimal, fractional (GCD-reduced), feet-inches. Metric modes: mm, cm. Settings UI: format pills, decimal places (0/1), fraction precision (1/4–1/64) in the gear dropdown between Units and Currency. **Key decisions**: (1) internal storage keeps full precision — `convertDim()` never rounds, `formatDim()` rounds for display only, enabling lossless round-trips (96.375" → 2447.925mm → 96.375"). (2) Auto-reset format mode on unit-system switch (imperial fractional → metric resets to mm; metric cm → imperial resets to decimal). (3) CSV export keeps raw numbers for machine readability. (4) `parseDim()` supersedes `parseVal()` for dimension inputs — handles feet-inches (`1' 3 3/8`), mixed fractions, unit suffixes. **Bug fixes during implementation**: `_toFeetInches` floating-point edge case (95.999... displayed as `7' 12"` instead of `8' 0"` — added carry normalization); `parseDim` feet-inches regex missed ASCII apostrophe (only had Unicode prime/curly); parsing order fixed to check feet-inches before stripping quotes. **Persistence**: `business_info.unit_format` jsonb column (migration applied), synced via `_saveUnitFormat()` → `saveBizInfo()`, loaded in `_applyBizInfoFromDB()`. **Verification**: typecheck clean, all format modes tested in dev preview, round-trip conversion verified lossless.

- 2026-05-07 — **Cabinet Builder UX & pricing refactor (batch 1, 8 items)**. Single pass across `src/cabinet.js` / `src/cabinet-calc.js` / `src/cabinet-render.js` / `src/cabinet-library.js` / `src/migrate.js` / `src/scheduler.js` / `src/app.js` / `src/orders.js` / `src/business.js` / `index.html`, plus 2 schema migrations. (1) **Contingency → % of labour time**: `cbSettings.contingencyHours` replaced by `cbSettings.contingencyPct` (default 5); `calcCBLine` and `calcCBSections` multiply `autoLabour` by `(1 + pct/100)` before converting to cost — both labour hours and labour cost reflect contingency at the per-cabinet level. The old per-order `orders.contingency_hours` plumbing is no longer read in scheduler.js / app.js's `_orderHoursBreakdown`; the order popup loses its standalone Contingency input (replaced with an info note pointing at My Rates) and the breakdown's "Cabinet labour" row now shows an "incl. N% contingency" tag. New columns added but not yet read for per-order overrides: `orders.contingency_pct`, `business_info.default_contingency_pct`. (2) **Packaging moved**: from Core Rates to Other Labour Times in My Rates (Core: 5 rates / Other: 6 rates). (3) **Power-law UI parity**: the existing per-type refHours math (live since 2026-05-05) is now exposed via two distinct sections — the Drawers section split into adjacent **Drawer Fronts** + **Drawer Boxes** collapsibles, each with their own type select / material / live cost. (5) **"Results" tab → "Project"**: label-only change in `index.html:261`; internal view key stays `'results'` to avoid churn across the carved files. (6) **Per-component finish**: standalone Finish section removed; new `doorFinish` / `drawerFrontFinish` / `drawerBoxFinish` fields on cabinet lines, each with its own picker inside the Cabinet/Doors/Drawer Fronts/Drawer Boxes sections. Pricing applies per-component surface area: carcass finish to `2HD + 2innerW·D + W·H`, door finish to `doorTotalArea`, drawer-front finish to `drawerFrontTotalArea`, drawer-box finish to per-box surface area. (7) **Per-component hardware (3 lists) + auto-hw removed**: standalone Hardware section gone; new `doorHwItems` / `drawerHwItems` arrays alongside the repurposed `hwItems` (now cabinet-only). The hardcoded `line.doors * 2 * 6` hinges and `line.drawers * 24` slides in cabinet-calc.js are deleted — hardware totals strictly from the three manual lists. `_smartCBHwSuggest` / `_smartCBHwAddSuggest` / `_addCBHwByName` / `_openNewCBHardwarePopup` / `_saveNewCBHardware` / `updateCBHw` / `removeCBHw` all gained an optional `scope` parameter (`'cabinet'` | `'door'` | `'drawer'`, default `'cabinet'` for back-compat); per-section DOM ids namespaced (`cb-hw-${scope}-${lineId}-${idx}`). New `_hwListKey` / `_hwList` helpers in cabinet.js. (8) **Cabinet qty stepper removed from sidebar**: deleted from the Cabinet section's first form-row in `renderCBEditor`; the existing qty stepper in the Project view's cabinet card remains the only place to edit qty post-add. **Schema**: migrations `cabinet_per_component_finish_hardware_and_contingency_pct` (5 columns on `quote_lines`: `door_finish text`, `drawer_front_finish text`, `drawer_box_finish text`, `door_hardware jsonb default '[]'`, `drawer_hardware jsonb default '[]'`; 1 column on `orders`: `contingency_pct numeric`) and `business_info_default_contingency_pct` (1 column: `default_contingency_pct numeric`). `migrate.js` `_quoteLineRowToCB` and `_cbLineToRow` extended to round-trip the new fields. `database.types.ts` regenerated. **Verification** (live in dev preview, signed in): typecheck clean; tab reads "Project"; sidebar Cabinet section row 1 shows Width/Height/Depth (no Qty); Core Rates 5 rows incl. Contingency at unit `%` default 5; Other Labour Times 6 rows incl. Packaging; calcCBLine ratio test = 1.20 hours and 1.20 cost when pct flips 0→20; per-component finish independent (cabinet £241.50 vs doors £57.64 with door-only Oil finish at £12/m²); hardware totals = `cabinet:10 + door:24 + drawer:96 = 130` with empty auto-hw; `cbSaveToLibrary` source contains `switchCBMainView('library')`; `cbCommitToProject` source contains `switchCBMainView('results')`; refHours per type intact (Carcass:Standard, Doors:Slab/Shaker/Vinyl-Wrapped/Integrated Handle, Drawer Fronts:Slab/Shaker, Drawer Boxes:Standard/Dovetail).

Eight-point overhaul of the editor sidebars driven by user feedback that line-item inputs read as a "jumble" and the schedule block was visually heavy. (1) **Line-item rows redesigned** — item + labour rows in `_orderLineRowHtml()` (`src/app.js`) and `_lineRowHtml()` switched from a single horizontal strip of unlabelled 56-px inputs to a two-line `.li-row-stacked` layout: row 1 has kind badge + name + amount + remove-button, row 2 has labelled fields (`Qty / Price / Hrs` for items, `Hours / Rate /hr` for labour) using new `.li-fields` / `.li-field` / `.li-num` classes. (2) **Compact inline rows** — Pricing and Schedule meta now use new `.pf-row-inline` + `.pf-inline` + `.pf-input-compact` utilities (`styles.css`): `Markup [20] %  Tax [13] %` sits on one line; same pattern for `Auto schedule` / `Priority` / `Run-over` / `Override hours` / `Allocated`. Replaces the chunky two-column `.pf-row` (label-above) layout. Date inputs get explicit `min-width: 130px; height: 24px;` so they match text-input rhythm. (3) **Manual start/end inputs removed** — the `<div id="po-manual-dates">` block (with `po-manual-start` + `po-manual-end`) deleted. Production Start (`po-start`) is now the single editable date when auto-schedule is off (disabled when on, picks up greyed `:disabled` styling). `saveOrderEditor` mirrors `production_start_date` into `manual_start_date` when `auto_schedule=false` (legacy column kept for back-compat) and writes `manual_end_date = null`. **Scheduler change** in `src/scheduler.js` manual-orders branch: when `manual_end_date` is null, walks the calendar from `manual_start_date || production_start_date` consuming `hoursRequired` per workday — same algorithm as auto-orders — to compute `endISO`. Existing rows with explicit `manual_end_date` still honour it. (4) **Disabled-date colour** — new `.pf-input:disabled` rule (`color: var(--muted); cursor: not-allowed`) plus `:disabled::-webkit-calendar-picker-indicator { opacity: 0.35 }` so the auto-driven date renders visibly greyed-out. (5) **Hours-allocated override** — new nullable column `orders.hours_allocated` (numeric). NULL = use the existing line-item-summed `orderHoursRequired()`; non-null = the scheduler reserves exactly that value. UI: new "Override hours" checkbox + Allocated input inside Schedule (visible only when checked); auto breakdown panel hides while override is on. `_orderHoursOverrideToggle()` in `src/orders.js` shows/hides the input + breakdown and seeds the input with the current computed total on enable. `orderHoursRequired()` (`src/scheduler.js`) early-returns the override value before any line-item computation; `_orderHoursBreakdown()` (`src/app.js`) does the same for the readout consistency. (6) **Schedule section collapsible** — wrapped in `<details class="editor-section editor-section--collapsible">` with `<summary>` showing title + 1-line state readout (`Auto · Start 12 May · 12.5 h` or `Manual · Start 14 May · 8.0 h`); open/closed state persisted in `localStorage['pc_order_sched_open']`, default closed. New `_renderOrderSchedSummary()` in `src/orders.js` reads live values from inputs and runs on every change. CSS hides the native `::-webkit-details-marker` and renders a custom `▾` chevron that rotates on open. (7) **Totals above schedule** — `<div class="pf-totals" id="po-totals">` moved from the bottom (under Notes) to immediately after Pricing inputs and before the Schedule `<details>`. Same reorder in quotes (totals between Pricing and Notes — quotes have no schedule section). (8) **Status + order # removed from project header** — calls to `_renderProjectHeader()` (`src/ui.js:178`) in both `renderOrderEditor()` and `renderQuoteEditor()` no longer pass `status` / `summary` fields. The `metaRow` (status pill + summary line) is omitted; project name + back button + client line remain. (4) **Discount column + whole-order discount** — new `discount` column (numeric, 0-100 percentage) on all four tables (`quotes`, `orders`, `quote_lines`, `order_lines`); also added `schedule_hours` to `quote_lines` for parity with `order_lines` (the new Hrs column on quote-side rows needs somewhere to write). `_lineSubtotal` (`src/quotes.js:130`) multiplies materials+labour by `(1 - discount/100)` so all downstream sums stay simple. `_renderOrderLineTotals` / `_renderQuoteLineTotals` add `(after-tax) × order_discount/100` as a separate red row between Tax and the final total, hidden when zero. (5) **Labour tile dropped from UI** — `_O_ICON_LABOUR` add-tile and `_qAddLine('labour')` add-tile removed from both editors; `.editor-add-tiles` grid switched from `repeat(3, ...)` to `repeat(2, ...)`. Existing `line_kind='labour'` rows in the DB still render in-place (mapped to item-style with `labour_hours` → Hrs cell; `_lineSubtotal`'s labour branch still computes `hrs × rate` for back-compat). `_orderLineAdd` / `_lineAdd` keep their `labour` branch defensively but no UI calls them now. (6) **PDFs** — quote print/PDF (`src/quotes.js:953-973` HTML, `src/cutlist.js:2147-2320` jspdf) + order PDFs (`src/cutlist.js:2512-2712` for order_confirmation/proforma/invoice) gain a `Disc%` column when `rows.some(r => r.discount > 0)` and a red `Discount (N%)` totals row when `q.discount > 0` / `o.discount > 0`. Both conditional — when no discounts exist, PDFs look exactly like before. (7) **CSV** — Quote CSV export header gains `Discount %`; importer reads `r[6]` as discount, shifts `status`/`date`/`notes` to `r[7]`/`r[8]`/`r[9]`. `updateQuoteField`'s `numFields` list adds `discount`. (8) **Migration** — `supabase/migrations/20260510233952_add_discount_columns.sql` adds the four `discount numeric default 0` columns plus `quote_lines.schedule_hours numeric default 0`. **MCP `apply_migration` was blocked by harness permissions; user to apply via Supabase SQL editor** before save paths can persist the new fields. **Code is migration-tolerant**: reads use `(o.discount ?? 0)`, the chip inputs default to 0, the totals row stays hidden, the per-line Disc% cell stays as `—`; save handlers always include the field but a write to a missing column will fail at the DB level (same pattern as the 2026-05-09 `hours_allocated` rollout). `npm run typecheck` clean. SCHEMA.md updated under §§ 3.14 / 3.15 / 3.16. Plan at `~/.claude/plans/clean-up-orders-dapper-yao.md`.
- 2026-05-11 — **Orders / Quotes editor port from mockup J (column toggles + stock library + per-order stock markup)**. Second-pass redesign of the order/quote editor sidebar, replacing the bridge from the 2026-05-10 pass with the J-mockup design the user iterated on extensively (`mockups/orders/orders-redesign-J-column-toggles.html` for orders, `quotes-redesign-J-column-toggles.html` for quotes). Major changes: (1) **New `.ed-head` editor header** with back-arrow + tab-icon + editable order/quote-number prefix (`#NNNN` / `#Q-NNNN`) + project name on row 1, client name + clickable status `<select>` styled as a coloured badge on row 2 (`data-status` attribute drives the CSS background colour per status). Order number input dropped the `#` prefix into a static `<span>` next to the input so the input value stays bare digits; quote number similarly dropped the `Q-` prefix and re-prepends it on save. (2) **Column-toggle pills** (`Discount` / `Hours` / `Stock`) added to a new `.cl-section-header` row above the line-items table, replacing the old `editor-section-title`. State persisted in `localStorage['pc_order_col_{disc,hrs,stock}']` and `pc_quote_col_*`. Toggling Disc/Hrs adds `.hide-disc`/`.hide-hrs` to the table so the corresponding columns hide via CSS; toggling Stock reveals the stock smart-library below the add buttons (no column). (3) **Line items table** — `_orderLineRowHtml` / `_lineRowHtml` (`src/app.js`) refactored: descriptions are now `<textarea class="cl-input desc">` with `_autoGrowTextarea` so they wrap onto multiple lines and the row height adapts; cells use the universal `.cl-input` class; the row template emits `col-handle / col-dot / col-desc / col-qty / col-price / col-hrs / col-disc / col-total / col-x`. Hrs column header + cells render in muted grey (`var(--muted)`, opacity 0.7 on the header) to telegraph that workshop hours are PDF-hidden; cabinet rows seed the Hrs cell with `calcCBLine().labourHrs × qty` and render it italic via `.is-computed` until the user edits it. (4) **Split add buttons** — `+ Cabinet` / `+ Item` replace the `editor-add-tiles` grid (`.cl-add-row` / `.cl-add-btn`). Plain text, no colour dots in the buttons. (5) **Stock smart-library** — when the Stock pill is on, a search input with a `+` button reveals below the add buttons. The `+` button calls `_openNewStockPopup()` (the canonical app.js helper — see (8) for disambiguation). Typing in the search renders the `.stock-suggest` dropdown grouped by stock category with sticky section labels; clicking a row pushes a new `line_kind='stock'` line via `_oAddStockLineFromLibrary` / `_qAddStockLineFromLibrary`. Implemented in new `_stockSearchRender(q, suggestId, onPick)` helper (`src/app.js`). Below the search: a single `Stock Markup [N]%` input persisted on the order/quote row's `stock_markup` column. (6) **Pricing chips refactored to Tax + Disc only** — the order/quote-level `markup` chip is removed from the UI. The legacy `markup` column on `quotes` / `orders` stays in the DB for back-compat; saves preserve whatever value was already there (rather than zero it out via the missing input), and the legacy markup still applies in totals math when non-zero on a pre-existing row. New `stock_markup` is the only user-facing markup field. Divider line moved from below the Pricing chips to ABOVE the Pricing header (`border-top: 1px solid var(--border)` on the section, `border-bottom: none`), giving a clear separation between the line-items / stock-library block and the pricing block. (7) **Totals math** — `_renderOrderLineTotals` / `_renderQuoteLineTotals` and `quoteTotal` updated: `_lineSubtotal` returns the same `{materials, labour}` shape per line, but the order/quote totals reducer now splits `stockMat` out so the stock_markup can be applied to stock-line materials only before the legacy markup → tax → discount chain. `orderTotalsFromLines` / `quoteTotalsFromLines` extended to return `stockMat` alongside `materials` / `labour`. New "Stock markup (N%)" row appears in the totals breakdown only when stock_markup × stockMat > 0. (8) **Footer buttons removed** from the editor — Delete / Work Order / Invoice / PDF / → Order live on the order/quote CARD in the main list, so the editor sidebar is editing-focused. A single `+ Create Order` / `+ Create Quote` button remains for the new-row flow. (9) **`_openNewStockPopup` disambiguation fix** — cabinet-library.js had a function named `_openNewStockPopup(fieldName)` that actually opened a "New Finish" popup, shadowing app.js's canonical new-stock popup due to script load order. Renamed it to `_openNewCBFinishPopup`; updated its 3 legitimate finish-popup callers (cabinet-render.js's `finishSmart`, cabinet-library.js `_smartRatesFinishSuggest` and `_smartCBFinishSuggest`). Side-effect fix: the cabinet builder's "Add new material" / "Add new edge banding to stock" buttons in `_smartRatesSheetSuggest` / `_smartRatesEdgeSuggest` / `_smartCBMaterialSuggest` (which were calling the misnamed function and erroneously opening a finish popup) now correctly invoke the real stock popup. (10) **Schema migration staged** at `supabase/migrations/20260511015625_stock_kind_and_markup.sql`: drops + re-creates the `line_kind` check constraint on `quote_lines` and `order_lines` to allow `'stock'` (existing values still valid); adds `stock_markup numeric not null default 0` to `quotes` and `orders`. MCP `apply_migration` blocked by harness permissions — user to apply manually via Supabase SQL editor; reads / saves are migration-tolerant until then (defaults to 0, no rows visible as kind=stock yet). The HTML print path in `printQuote` and the jspdf builders `_buildQuotePDF` + `_buildOrderDocPDF` (`src/cutlist.js`) all add a "Stock markup (N%)" row in the totals block, between Subtotal and the legacy Markup row, only when `stock_markup × stockMat > 0`. `npm run typecheck` clean.
